		var xrxRemoveValue = function(list, value, separator) {
		  separator = separator || ",";
		  var values = list.split(separator);
		  for(var i = 0 ; i < values.length ; i++) {
		    if(values[i] == value) {
		      values.splice(i, 1);
		      return values.join(separator);
		    }
		  }
		  return list;
		}

// Metrics events

Coveo.$$(searchPageRoot).on("changeAnalyticsCustomData", function(e, args) {
	var coveoEvent = args.actionType+"-"+args.actionCause;
	if (xrx_is_debug) {
		console.log("Coveo filter event: "+coveoEvent);
		console.log(args);
	}

	if (coveoEvent == "interface-interfaceChange") {
		coveoEvent = "int-tab-"+args.originLevel2.toLowerCase();
	} else if (coveoEvent == "resultsLayout-changeResultsLayout") {
		coveoEvent = "int-layout-"+args.metaObject.resultsLayoutChangeTo.toLowerCase();
	} else if (coveoEvent == "misc-resultsSort") {
		coveoEvent = "int-sort-"+args.metaObject.resultsSortBy.toLowerCase();
	} else if (coveoEvent == "document-documentField") {
		coveoEvent = "int-type-"+args.metaObject.facetValue.toLowerCase();
	} else if (coveoEvent == "breadcrumb-breadcrumbFacet") {
		coveoEvent = "int-type-close";
	} else if (coveoEvent == "breadcrumb-breadcrumbResetAll") {
		coveoEvent = "int-clear";
	} else if (coveoEvent == "document-documentQuickview") {
		coveoEvent = "int-quick-view";
	} else if (coveoEvent == "facet-facetSelect") {
		coveoEvent = "int-filter-"+args.metaObject.facetTitle.toLowerCase()+"-"+args.metaObject.facetValue.toLowerCase();
	} else if (coveoEvent == "facet-facetDeselect") {
		coveoEvent = "int-filter-deselect";
	} else if (coveoEvent == "facet-facetClearAll") {
		coveoEvent = "int-filter-clear all";
	} else if (coveoEvent == "facet-facetUpdateSort") {
		coveoEvent = "int-filter-sort-"+args.metaObject.facetTitle.toLowerCase()+"-"+args.metaObject.criteria.toLowerCase();
	} else if (coveoEvent == "getMoreResults-pagerNumber") {
		coveoEvent = "page-"+args.metaObject.pagerNumber;
	} else if (coveoEvent == "getMoreResults-pagerPrevious") {
		coveoEvent = "prev";
	} else if (coveoEvent == "getMoreResults-pagerNext") {
		coveoEvent = "next";
	} else if (coveoEvent == "getMoreResults-pagerResize") {
		coveoEvent = "results-"+args.metaObject.currentResultsPerPage;
	} else if (coveoEvent == "interface-searchFromLink") {
		// search from link
		return;
	} else if (coveoEvent == "omnibox-omniboxAnalytics" || coveoEvent == "box-searchboxSubmit") {
		// search refinement in page
		s.events = s.apl(s.events,"event18",",",2);
		return;
	} else {
		// no metrics for you
		return;
	}

	if (window.xrx_sc_synthetic_lid_event) {
		xrx_sc_synthetic_lid_event(coveoEvent);
  } else {
    console.log('xrx_sc_synthetic_lid_event not available');
  }


});

// paint search results, part of metrics
Coveo.$$(searchPageRoot).on("newResultsDisplayed", function(e, args) {

	if (xrxCoveoFirstPaint && typeof window.performance == 'object') {
		var painted = new Date().getTime();
		var coveoPerf = {
			"navigation-to-fetch": performance.timing.fetchStart - performance.timing.navigationStart,
			"fetch-to-response": performance.timing.responseEnd - performance.timing.fetchStart,
			"response-to-results": painted - performance.timing.responseEnd,
			"navigation-to-results": painted - performance.timing.navigationStart
		};

		var dataPacket = {
			'application': 'coveoPerf',
			'coveo-performance': coveoPerf,
			'locale-string': digitalData.locale.locale,
			'search-hub': Coveo.Analytics.options.searchHub.defaultValue,
			'tier': digitalData.locale.tier
		};

		var logglypixel = document.createElement('img');
    logglypixel.src = "https://logs-01.loggly.com/inputs/7cabc394-8e60-4bf9-8d74-f98ec1a89df9/tag/coveoPerf/1*1.gif?PLAINTEXT="+escape(JSON.stringify(dataPacket));
  	console.log(dataPacket);
	}


	// identify no search results case
	//if (e.target.CoveoResultList.currentlyDisplayedResults.length == 0) {
		// empty results
	//	s.events = s.apl(s.events,"event47",",",2);
	//} else {
		// otherwise remove event from list since it's sticky across search refinements
	//	s.events = xrxRemoveValue(s.events,"event47");
	//}
	if (xrxCoveoFirstPaint) {
		xrxCoveoFirstPaint= false;
		xrxCoveoInitializeMetrics();
	}

	// check input box to see if search term has changed
	var xrxCoveoSearchTerm = document.querySelector(".CoveoOmnibox input").value;
	if (xrxCoveoSearchTerm != xrxCoveoLastSearchTerm) {
		xrxCoveoLastSearchTerm = xrxCoveoSearchTerm;
		xrxCoveoNewSearchTerm(xrxCoveoLastSearchTerm);
	}

	// add handlers to results links being painted
  for (var i = 0; i < e.target.lastChild.children.length; i++) {
    var currentResult = e.target.lastChild.children[i];
		if (currentResult.CoveoResult) {
      var element = currentResult.children[0].querySelector("div.coveo-result-cell > a.CoveoResultLink");
      if (element !== null) {
	      element.setAttribute('data-sequence',currentResult.CoveoResult.index+1);
	      element.setAttribute('data-title',currentResult.CoveoResult.Title);
	      element.setAttribute('data-lid','rank'+element.getAttribute('data-sequence')+"-"+element.getAttribute('data-title'));
      }
		}
  }

  if (xrx_is_debug) {
  	console.log("Coveo results painted");
  }



});

// end metrics

		Coveo.init(searchPageRoot)

		searchPageRoot.addEventListener("afterComponentsInitialization", function () {
		  var analytics = document.querySelector('.CoveoAnalytics');
		  if (analytics != null) {
		    Coveo.get(analytics).setOriginContext('Hosted');
		  }
		});



		var supportLang = "English";
		var supportShortLang = "en";
		var shortLang = digitalData.locale['url-prefix'].substr(0,2);
		var langMap = {
			"de": "German",
			"es": "Spanish",
			"fr": "French",
			"it": "Italian",
			"pt": "Portuguese"
			// all else is English
		};

		if (langMap[shortLang]) {
			supportLang = langMap[shortLang];
			supportShortLang = shortLang;
		}

		var customContext = {
			"locale": digitalData.locale['url-prefix'],
			"lang": shortLang,
			"fulllang": digitalData.locale.language,
			"product": "",
			"supportlang": supportLang,
			"supportshortlang": supportShortLang
		}

		searchPageRoot.addEventListener("buildingQuery", function(e) {
			e.detail.queryBuilder.addContext(customContext);
   	});

		var currentPage = 'XeroxSupport';
		var currentLocation = encodeURIComponent(window.location.pathname+window.location.hash);

	})

function resultFixer(result) {
  resultPropFixer(result, 'ClickUri');
  resultPropFixer(result, 'PrintableUri');
  resultPropFixer(result, 'clickUri');
  resultPropFixer(result, 'Uri');
  resultPropFixer(result, 'printableUri');

  resultPropFixer(result.raw, 'clickableuri');
  resultPropFixer(result.raw, 'sysclickableuri');

  resultPropFixer(result.raw, 'printableuri');
  resultPropFixer(result.raw, 'sysprintableuri');

  resultPropFixer(result.raw, 'uri');
  resultPropFixer(result.raw, 'sysuri');
}

function resultPropFixer(rawResult, prop) {
  var locale = digitalData.locale['url-prefix'];
  var tmpLink = rawResult[prop];

  if (tmpLink) {
    if (locale !== 'en-us') {
      tmpLink = tmpLink.replace('en-us', locale);
    }

    rawResult[prop] = tmpLink;
  }
}

}

<script class="result-template" id="Card" type="text/underscore" data-layout="card">
<%
        var xrx_locale_link = raw.sysclickableuri;
        if (raw.source == "Xerox Support" || raw.source == "Xerox Support D&D") {
            xrx_locale_link = raw.sysclickableuri.replace(/[a-z]{4}\.html/,'enus.html');
        } else {
            xrx_locale_link = raw.sysclickableuri;
            var article_matches = xrx_locale_link.match(/support\/article\/([a-z]{2})\/([0-9]+)$/);
            if (article_matches !== null) {
                var article_language = article_matches[1];
                var article_id = article_matches[2];
                xrx_locale_link = 'https://www.support.xerox.com/en-us/article/'+article_language+"/"+article_id;
            }

        }
%>
    <div class="coveo-result-frame">

        <div class="coveo-result-row">
            <div class="coveo-result-cell coveo-icon-cell" >
                <span class="CoveoIcon" data-small="true" data-with-label="false"></span>
            </div>
            <div class="coveo-result-cell coveo-title-cell">
				<a class="CoveoResultLink coveo-result-title" href="<%= xrx_locale_link %>"><%= raw.heading ? raw.heading : raw.title %></a>
			</div>
        </div>
        <div class="coveo-result-cell coveo-result-cell" style="vertical-align: top;padding-left: 16px;">
            <div class="coveo-result-row">
                <div class="coveo-result-cell">
                    <span class="CoveoFieldValue coveo-result-data coveo-with-label" data-field="@filetitle"></span>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="coveo-result-row">
                <div class="coveo-result-cell">
                    <span class="CoveoFieldValue coveo-result-data coveo-with-label" data-field="@messagetext"></span>
                </div>
            </div>
